## 词性 AUX (17 words)

1. __be__ /biː/ （用来说明人、事物或状态，表示性质、状态、工作等） used to say something about a person, thing, or state, to show a permanent or temporary quality, state, job, etc. （2225 次） 
	- My name `is` Richard Stewart. 

1. __do__ /də/ （与另一动词连用构成疑问句和否定句，包括表示禁止的命令，有时因文体原因亦可用于肯定句） used with another verb to form questions and negative sentences, including negative orders, and sometimes in affirmative sentences for reasons of style （681 次） 
	- And where `do` you live? 

1. __will__ /wɪl/ **将**，将要 used to talk about what is going to happen in the future, especially things that you are certain about or things that are planned （397 次） 
	- We`'ll` be looking for your book. 

1. __can__ /kæn/ **能**，会 to be able to （211 次） 
	- `Can` I help you? 

1. __would__ /wʊd/ （从过去的角度指将来发生的事）将，将要 used to refer to future time from the point of view of the past （179 次） 
	- `Would` you like some coffee? 

1. __could__ /kʊd/ （can 的过去式，表示能够或允许）能，可以 past simple of "can", used to talk about what someone or something was able or allowed to do （62 次） 
	- He couldn't take time off to come to New York with me. 

1. __should__ /ʃʊd/ **应当**，应该 used to say or ask what is the correct or best thing to do （46 次） 
	- You `should` take the number 1 subway. 

1. __must__ /mʌst/ **必须** used to show that it is necessary or very important that something happens in the present or future （31 次） 
	- And you `must` be Susan. 

1. __may__ /meɪ/ （表示可能性）可能，也许 used to express possibility （19 次） 
	- `May` I take a picture of you and your little boy? 

1. __might__ /maɪt/ （may 的过去式）可能，可以 past simple of the verb may, used especially when reporting what someone has said, thought, asked, etc. （17 次） 
	- It `might` be a little cold. 

1. __'ve(或许是 I've?)__    （4 次） 
	- You must`'ve` come home very late. 

1. __ought__ /ˈɔːt ˌtə/ （表示做某事有必要、值得或有利）应该，应当 used to show when it is necessary or would be a good thing to perform the activity referred to by the following verb （4 次） 
	- You really `ought` to take some time off.

	- Oh, I was sorry to hear about your wife `having` passed away.

	- `Shall` we go?

	- Somebody `else'll` buy it by then.

	- My niece is `getting` married, and I've been trying to find just the right thing for her.

## 词性 CCONJ (5 words)

	- Oh, it's not finished yet, `but` I have some of the pictures.

	- You ordered enough for three `or` four people, but I'm not complaining.

	- You get one point for each letter, `plus` the person with the longest word gets ten extra points. 

1. __n__ /en/ （英语字母表的第14个字母） the 14th letter of the English alphabet （1 次） 
	- Some rock '`n`' roll.

## 词性 SCONJ (12 words)

1. __how__ /haʊ/ **如何**，怎么 in what way, or by what methods （129 次）

	- `When` did you come here?

	- `Why` not? 

1. __where__ /weər/ **去哪里**;在哪里 to, at, or in what place （37 次） 
	- And `where` do you live? 

1. __before__ /bɪˈfɔːr/ **在…之前**;以前 at or during a time earlier than (the thing mentioned) （23 次） 
	- You need to complete some forms `before` the class. 

1. __because__ /bɪˈkəz/ **因为**，由于 for the reason that （21 次） 
	- She's unhappy `because` she's had to go to Chicago on a business trip and can't leave till tonight. 

1. __till__ /tɪl/ **直到**;到…为止 up to (the time that); until （11 次） 
	- She's unhappy because she's had to go to Chicago on a business trip and can't leave `till` tonight. 

1. __since__ /sɪns/ **此后**，从此 from a particular time in the past until a later time, or until now （8 次） 
	- Yes, I think it's important for me to be there `since` her mother died. 

1. __except__ /ɪkˈsept/ （表示不包括）除…之外 not including; but not （3 次） 
	- `Except` for my grandfather. 

1. __wherever__ /weəˈrev.ər/ **无论到（**或在）哪里;无论什么地方 to or in any or every place （1 次） 
	- I'll make new friends `wherever` we are as long as we're together. 

1. __whether__ /ˈweð.ər/ （尤用于转述问题或表达疑问）是否 (used especially in reporting questions and expressing doubts) if, or not （1 次） 
	- I've been wrestling with the question of `whether` I go back to work or not.
